Current Affairs Commentary

When Will Unanimity Against Foreign Aggression Arrive? 36

Since the Japanese army's atrocities occurred, half a month has passed in an instant. Enemy cavalry roar and Japanese flags flutter. Thirty million compatriots in the Northeast have fallen under the enemy's trampling hooves. More than four million square miles of territory have been shattered by violence. Gazing into the distance at the Northeast, smoke signals cover the land, and a foul atmosphere obscures the sky. We are not all dead yet, and the national spirit still exists here. We should all embrace a resolution to die fighting, to promote our national spirit and reclaim our rivers and mountains.

Currently, the people of the whole country, farmers, merchants, students, are eager to take action, eagerly awaiting, morning and night, the central and Guangdong authorities to issue countermeasures for unified resistance. Enemy hatred and shared anger, the people's spirit is at its peak. Today's matter can be decided in one sentence: only resisting Japan can save the country, and only unanimous resistance to external aggression can save the country. Internal disputes must absolutely not be allowed to continue. At this moment, survival is at stake. There is no room for delay. The people of the country must cast aside all doubts and resentments, change their ways and repent of their mistakes with sincere, ardent blood, rise up together, and unite against foreign aggression. There is nothing else to say. If there were, there would be no way to face the country or the people.

The party is subordinate to the country, so it must first save the country. The party's foundation is the people, so it should especially save the people first. Now that the country is in danger and the people are suffering, yet they are still bickering over partisan disputes and abandoning the current major task of saving the country, this is misleading the country with partisan views, sacrificing the country for partisan views. The country is jointly owned by all our people, and the people will never sit idly by and watch it sink. If there are those who harm the national foundation, all the people of the country should rise up and abandon them together.

Today's matter requires those who resolutely rise up based on the Three Principles of the People and guide the people to the path of resisting Japan and saving the country to be the people's mentors and loved by the people. All eyes are watching, not missing a detail. If, at this time of national crisis, they are still bickering over partisan disputes and forgetting the current national crisis, they will lose the people's hearts. Where will they then rely? The country will perish. Where will they then attach themselves? The people of the country should most earnestly recognize this.

The past is like the past dead. The future is like the future born. The roar of iron cavalry is the alarm bell awakening us from our deep sleep. The current foreign troubles are the driving force for our national rejuvenation and self-strengthening. It is said that "a country without foreign enemies will always perish." At this time, all our citizens should firmly grasp this opportunity and rise up to fight. Party and government leaders, as representatives of the people, should especially stand on the front lines of the people and lead the way. Those who violate this intention are abandoning their responsibilities and will not be tolerated by all the people of the country.

Domestic Urgent Telegrams Two

Anti-Japanese National Salvation Movement 37

(Nanjing) The Capital's All-Circles Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association began a general registration of Japanese goods on the 4th. More than 20 stores in the city have already registered on the list. On the same day, the Japanese goods inspection office in Xiaguan seized many pieces of Japanese woolens of various colors at the Jinghu Railway Station and immediately detained them. (4th Special Telegram)

(Nanjing) The inspection department of the Capital's All-Circles Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association discovered that the Daofeng and Yuantai silk shops were selling Japanese goods. In addition to confiscating the goods, it was decided to parade the shop staff as a warning on the morning of the 5th. (4th Special Telegram)

(Nanjing) The Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association of the Central Political School organized 40 propaganda teams, each with 10 people. On the 4th, they took 30,000 copies of paintings, leaflets, slogans, etc., and went to the nearby rural areas to expand their propaganda. (4th Special Telegram)

(Nanjing) The military training division of the Jinling University Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association has established a battalion headquarters, divided into four companies, one independent company, and a special service team. Wang Rong, a military instructor at the school, has been hired as the battalion commander and has begun training. Field exercises are held once every Sunday. (4th Special Telegram)

(Nanjing) The party-affiliated staff of the Judicial Yuan, the Department of Judicial Administration, and the Supreme Court have formed an Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association to connect with national judicial circles to organize themselves voluntarily. (4th Special Telegram)

(Nanjing) All members of the Central University Volunteer Army Rescue Team held their first general meeting on the 4th to discuss the organizational methods and educational plans, and Professor He Jiong gave a speech on party affairs. (4th Special Telegram)

(Nanjing) The China Youth Anti-Japanese National Salvation Corps held a swearing-in ceremony for all members at the Jiangsu People's Education Hall on the 4th. 237 members were present. It was stipulated that the corps flag would take on the meaning of iron and blood, using black and red colors. The 11th was designated as the corps' general propaganda day. A military committee was established to be responsible for training the Iron and Blood Volunteer Army. (4th Special Telegram)

(Nanjing) The Capital's All-Schools Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association decided to hold its fourth executive committee meeting on the 5th to discuss proposals such as promoting peaceful unification and unifying the organization of the volunteer armies of various schools. (4th Special Telegram)

(Nanjing) The joint office of the Capital's Anti-Japanese National Salvation Volunteer Army held its inaugural meeting on the 4th, electing standing directors and directors of the general affairs and assessment departments, and hiring several military advisors to be responsible for military training. (4th Special Telegram)

(Beiping) Fellow refugees from the Northeast organized an anti-Japanese association in Beiping and sent representatives to various provinces and regions, including Jing, Hu, Min, and Yue, to report on the Japanese atrocities in Shenyang and other places. Wang Huayi and Yan Yuheng, representatives of Yue and Hu, have departed one after the other. The representatives of other provinces and regions will set off immediately after the candidates are determined. (4th Special Telegram)

(Nanchang) All the teachers and staff went to the acting commander's office and the provincial government yesterday to petition for (1) preparing to declare war on Japan, (2) requesting the central government to withdraw from the League of Nations, (3) ordering Vice-Marshal Zhang to recover the lost territory, and (4) issuing firearms to the volunteer army. He Jian personally met them and promised to forward the request to the central government for approval. (4th Special Telegram)

(Nanchang) All elementary schools in the city were organized into four major brigades to promote anti-Japanese sentiment. The city party headquarters will go to various rural villages to promote propaganda today. (4th Special Telegram)

(Nanchang) The various schools have established three major volunteer army brigades to prepare for fighting against Japan. All teachers and staff will receive military training. Female students will learn nursing, and male students will all enlist. (4th Special Telegram)

(Anqing) The Provincial Reorganization Committee will hold an anti-Japanese national salvation propaganda week starting on the 4th and has scheduled a citizens' assembly for the 10th. (4th Special Telegram)

(Hankou) The action department inspection team of the Anti-Japanese Association is ready and will set off on the 5th to inspect Japanese goods. (4th Special Telegram)

(Changsha) The National Salvation Association decided to burn all confiscated enemy goods. A costumed performance will be held on the 10th. Japanese sailors have been parading with canes in groups of three or five for several days, intending to provoke. He Jian issued a history of national humiliation, ordering his subordinates to learn from the shame and prepare for war. The elementary schools in Changsha have established an Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association. (4th Special Telegram)

(Beiping) Representatives from Tsinghua University visited Zhang Xuezhong today, requesting the dispatch of a company of troops stationed in Xiyuan to teach the school's National Salvation Volunteer Army how to drill and use firearms. Wen Nianzhong met them on behalf of Zhang and agreed to the request. (4th Special Telegram)

Hunan Generals Send a Joint Telegram Declaring War on Japan 38

(Changsha) The generals in central Hunan jointly sent out a telegram to declare war on Japan. The original text is as follows: To the editors of various newspapers: We believe that China has been struck by heavenly misfortune, with banditry not yet quelled, followed by natural disasters, while the Japanese imperialists, based on their traditional and consistent continental policy, rejoice in our misfortune and take advantage of our peril, willing to be the leaders of aggression. Since the day of the September 18th Incident, they have dispatched troops to the Northeast, forcibly occupied our territory, massacred our compatriots, burned our government offices, and insulted our border officials. All kinds of tyrannical and violent actions have been fully exposed. The seriousness of the matter is by no means comparable to ordinary diplomatic issues. The only way to deal with it is to formally declare war, for there is no other way to save the nation. If our people's hearts are not yet completely dead, instead of emulating the Korean patriots, seeking to restore the country in the future, why not take advantage of the remaining breath and risk death to repay the country? The universe is vast and not entirely without justice. We must first have the determination to prefer to be shattered like jade, and then we will have countries that uphold justice and speak out for us. If we cannot swear to die ourselves, and yet want others to rescue us from death, there is no such thing in the world. I, Jian, await punishment on the battlefield and have a duty to defend the country. Holding spears and wearing armor, I will not hesitate to die ten thousand times. I humbly beg that our central government make a quick decision and implement a declaration of war against Japan. If we win the war, it will be enough to save the nation and the country from danger. Even if we unfortunately lose, it will forever leave glory to the nation and the country. Disaster is imminent, and there is no time to choose words. My sincere heart hopes to be carefully considered. Fourth Route Army Commander He Jian, Chief of Staff Liu Yinggu, Army Commander Liu Jianxu, Division Commanders Wang Dongyuan, Peng Weiren, Li Jue, Tao Guang, Chen Guangzhong, Chen Quzhen, Zhang Ying, and all officers and soldiers jointly kowtow with respect. (2nd Special Telegram)

(Changsha) Hunan Provincial Chairman He Jian and all committee members sent a telegram to the central government yesterday, stating: Urgent to the Nanjing Central Party Headquarters, National Government Chairman Chiang, Commander-in-Chief Chiang, Premier of the Executive Yuan, President of the Legislative Yuan, President of the Judicial Yuan, President of the Examination Yuan, President of the Control Yuan, Deputy Commander Zhang in Beiping, and Commander-in-Chief He of the Nanchang Forward Command: The Japanese bandits have already occupied the eastern provinces and are plotting to invade the south. Upon hearing the news, we are filled with unparalleled grief and indignation. The Japanese bandits are suffering from internal strife and external isolation and are eager to appease their people through invasion and plunder and to demonstrate their power to the world. They also fear that our unification will be completed and that there will be no opportunity to take advantage of us. Therefore, taking advantage of the remnants of our communist bandits and the extreme cruelty of natural disasters, they act against reason and justice to achieve their aims. It is absolutely impossible to salvage the situation with the diplomatic methods of the past. Our country's appeal to the League of Nations and various friendly nations, so that the world community will know the truth, is a necessary step. However, putting meat into a tiger's mouth will not make it spit it out unless you grab its throat. The public discussions of the League of Nations cannot make the Japanese people feel fearful, but rather they will take the opportunity to make various excuses to delay the withdrawal of their troops. Even if they withdraw, we are only begging for mercy from the enemy, exposing all our weaknesses, like a foolish person inviting a bully into his home, destroying his family and treating him politely. Disaster will come soon. How can we have the face to stand as a nation in the world? Thinking of the consequences, carefully considering the situation, the only option today is war. There is no second option. The people and soldiers love their country and have long shared a common hatred. If we can defend against insults and save the country, the internal strife will cease. There is no need for further exhortation. Our war equipment is well-prepared, although not as good as Japan's, but we are holding on to every strategic point. The danger has not yet been completely lost. With reason on our side, we will be strong. In the distant past, Wu and Jin repelled the armies of Qian and Qin. More recently, Turkey resisted Greece. There are many examples of the weak defeating the strong. If we can stand on our own, the world will surely have those who uphold justice and provide assistance. If we issue an order immediately, mobilizing the whole country, arming everyone, dividing into teams for training, and rotating to go to war, using defense as offense, we can destroy Japan in ten years. How can we say that we will win? Jian, having been a soldier for half his life, is moved by righteous indignation. In addition to ordering all schools in this province to organize and train according to the Volunteer Army Education Outline, all people over the age of twenty will practice martial arts, and all cities and counties will compile registers of retired soldiers and investigate useful military supplies for the practical use of the country. In addition, we will organize National Salvation Lecture Groups to widely encourage the people and repeatedly warn them to advance calmly and not be impatient. The 4th Route Army, with 100,000 soldiers in its divisions, brigades, regiments, and police, can serve as the vanguard on the appointed day. Hunan Province has 300,000 retired soldiers who can be conscripted into the reserve force. After April, the number will increase fivefold. The survival of the nation depends on this one action. We humbly offer our sincere advice and hope that you will carefully consider and instruct us to comply. (2nd Special Telegram)

(Hong Kong) Chen Mingshu and Li Wenfan arrived in Hong Kong at noon on the 3rd. Sun Ke, Wu Chaoshu, Chen Ce, Zhang Huichang, and Xiang Hanping arrived together. At that time, Chen, Huang, and Zhang discussed the situation in Guangxi for a long time, and a satisfactory solution had already been reached. Chen Mingshu returned to the Peninsula Hotel at 11 o'clock and was about to take the President Coolidge to Shanghai when he suddenly received a long-distance call from Zhang and Cai from the province, stating that Chiang had already replied by telegram with concrete solutions to various matters, and that Chen and Li's trip north could be suspended and that they would return to the province to discuss everything, etc. Therefore, Chen and Li returned to the province by early train on the morning of the 4th with Sun Ke. Deng Shizeng also traveled with them. Huang Jusu, under Chen Mingshu's orders, went to Shanghai early on the 4th. Chen Ce, Zhang Huichang, and Xiang Hanping returned to the province on the evening of the 4th. Chen, Li, Sun, and others arrived in the province at noon on the 4th and went to Tuisiyuan to continue talking with key figures in Guangdong, which did not end until 4 o'clock. (4th Special Telegram)

The telegram concerning this side was considered to require modification of the wording, and in addition, the Guangdong side has proposed many other conditions in recent days, which is inconsistent with the original agreement before Cai, Zhang, and Chen went to Guangdong. Therefore, a limit was set yesterday and a reply was sent to Cai and Zhang. It is heard that Chen Mingshu has left Hong Kong and will arrive tomorrow. Chen is only participating in the negotiations and does not hold the title of representative. After Chen returns to Nanjing, he will report on the successive meetings in Guangzhou and transfer his department, Jiang Guangnai's division, to the Nanjing-Shanghai line to take over the defense. As for the Guangdong side's negotiations, they will still be presided over by Cai and Zhang, who will communicate at any time. (4th Special Telegram)

Also, the Central Government sent a telegram to Cai and Zhang on the 2nd regarding the peace plan, but the content is not yet at the stage of being released. (4th Special Telegram)

(Nanjing) Hu Hanmin said to others that peaceful unification is the most urgent requirement at present, but as long as it is beneficial to the party and the country, he will never hold any preconceived notions. Now that foreign insults are imminent, party and government authorities should not make too many changes. (4th Special Telegram)

Japanese Commercial Panic 58

Heavy Blows to Both China and India

Japanese Government Attempts to Provide Financial Relief

Dentsu, Tokyo, 4th: Due to the spread of the anti-Japanese movement of the Chinese National Salvation Association and the UK's suspension of the gold standard, the pound's value plummeted, and Japanese trade with China and India has suffered heavy blows. As a result of yesterday's discussions between Finance Minister Inoue, Governor of the Bank of Japan Hijikata, and General Manager of Yokohama Specie Bank Oura, the Japanese government decided to provide financial relief to traders with China and India through the Bank of Japan and the Yokohama Specie Bank in the following ways: (1) For bills that have matured but cannot be delivered, the Yokohama Specie Bank may provide financial relief with the goods as collateral. (2) If the price is lower than the price when the invoice was issued due to the decline in the pound's value, the Yokohama Specie Bank will not require additional collateral. (3) It is customary to increase interest rates when swapping bills, but this time, due to the changes in the gold and silver ratio caused by the anti-Japanese movement and the decline in the pound's value, swapping must be done at the same interest rate. (4) If the Yokohama Specie Bank lacks relief funds, the Bank of Japan will provide support funds.

Major Developments in British Political Situation 59

Liberal Party Shows Internal Divisions

Reuters, London, 3rd: The Liberal Party previously intended to recognize tariffs, but its attitude suddenly became stronger shortly thereafter. Party leader George, who is currently ill in bed, does not approve of elections or tariffs. This is also one of the reasons why party members have suddenly changed their attitude. Acting party leader Samuel explained the situation to a joint meeting of directors of various Liberal Party organizations today. The meeting then passed a motion opposing the proposal for a general tariff, still advocating free trade, and expressing confidence in Samuel. After hearing this motion, Sir Simon, the most famous figure in the Liberal Party, told a Reuters interviewer that discussions on the election platform have almost reached the final stage. Many other Liberal Party members feel that the path that the nation should take is to trust the Prime Minister. For this reason, another organization has now been formed immediately. If so, there will be a major split within the Liberal Party. It is rumored that George is now planning to resign as party leader. The Conservative Party's opinion is also gradually strengthening, believing that a small number of Liberal Party members cannot be allowed to obstruct the policies of the National Government. Therefore, before Parliament adjourns on October 7, there may be major developments in the political situation.

British Lord Cecil

Austrian Parliament Passes Austerity Bill 62

Foreign Loan Expected to Succeed

National Citizen Daily, Vienna, 3rd: The Parliament tonight passed the national salary reduction bill with 165 votes against 8 in the third reading. Prime Minister Breche declared that Austria's finances were thus out of the crisis, as this was a condition for the new loan guaranteed by the League of Nations. The bill, which was in the midst of a storm, has been in progress for 24 hours. Prime Minister Breche has been working between parties, urging them to support the bill. After 24 hours without rest, it has finally been achieved. The bill stipulates a large-scale reduction of civil servants, reduction of official salaries, and an increase in taxes on beer, sugar, and oil. It is reported that all parties will soon organize a coalition cabinet to implement the bill.

Please Be Vigilant Against Fake Zhang · Qi · Yun 64

The Japanese's Preposterous Theory of the Zhonghe State

There is a popular saying in the Shanghai business community: "Not afraid of not knowing the goods, only afraid of comparing goods." In the future, they can turn falsehood into truth and transform themselves. If this secret is not exposed, the opening day of the so-called Zhonghe State will be the day of the loss of the three eastern provinces. The situation of the three eastern provinces can be regarded as half of China's territory. If the Northeast is lost, China will certainly not be able to survive in peace. It is bound to perish together. Therefore, if the Northeast is lost, China will also be lost. This is the extremely sinister and vicious trick of the Japanese.

What facts can be used to prove that the establishment of the so-called Zhonghe State is equivalent to the destruction of the three eastern provinces? Because the Japanese have a lot of experience in this kind of counterfeiting tricks. At the end of the European War, the victorious countries had long wanted to divide the colonies of Germany and other countries. The dispute had already begun. At that time, US President Wilson advocated the idea of not ceding land, which made it impossible to step down. Japan, one of the five powers, came out to offer advice. In the past, Japan had a scholar who was well-versed in law and reason, who wrote a theory of Korean mandate governance. Later, wasn't the Korean problem solved in this way? The term "mandate governance" is very respectable, and it is also just and humane. The Paris Peace Conference actually adopted it. This was the Japanese's proudest stroke after the war. In fact, those powerful countries that were entrusted with the mandate regarded those areas under mandate as their own territories. They were not polite at all. It was just a disguised form of cession. Now, the Zhonghe State that the Japanese want to successfully promote is located under their absolute military superiority. What can't they get with violent oppression? Public opinion can be raped, and representatives can be impersonated. Then, the so-called Zhonghe State will certainly become a state under mandate governance. As I said just now, mandate governance is equal to cession of land, and Zhonghe State is equal to mandate governance. Isn't the result that China's territory is transformed into Japan's territory?

What facts can be used to determine that the three eastern provinces are half of China's territory? If the Northeast is lost, China will be finished? This can be observed from three aspects: weather, geography, and people.

(A) Weather: The climate in the Northeast is generally dry. The mind and body are refreshed and suitable for health. Although the winter is cold, the summer temperature is high and there is more rain. The development of crops is therefore good. There are no strong winds and rainstorms in autumn. There is almost no year of poor harvest. We can see the grace of the weather from the fact that we can grow rice in the Northeast. But once you get west of the Datong Road, you can see deserts and camels. Because the rain in the Northeast comes from the Pacific Ocean. It gradually decreases from east to west, connecting to the Mongolian desert. Therefore, the Northeast is the only treasure trove on the Chinese border. The natural environment is still above the Yellow River basin. The northwest region is even more out of reach.

(B) Geography: The terrain in the Northeast is very complex. There are plains, hills, mountain ranges, and towering mountains. Plains produce large amounts of grain. Soybeans account for more than 60% of the world's total. In addition, there are countless wheat, sorghum, and corn. In short, the production capacity of the Northeast can feed twice the current population. The hills are the main mineral production areas. Centered on Shenyang, coal mines, iron mines, non-metals (except coal), and metals (except iron) are densely distributed. It is truly gold everywhere. The mountains have great forests. Towering old trees are lush and green. There are also high mountains and flowing water, which can also be used. The waterfall of Jingpo Lake is especially an infinite source of benefits. In addition, along the coast, there are more benefits of fish and salt. Therefore, the Japanese once said that Japan now imports 700 million yuan of raw materials from foreign countries every year. Once they get the Northeast, they can get whatever they want. They can attack and defend. They can be completely independent economically. At that time, China will not be able to punish their atrocities by economic sanctions. This is a major loss.

(C) People: The farmers in the Northeast are all immigrants from Shandong. They have traveled long distances and endured hardships. Therefore, the people are full of vitality and extremely lovable. According to what we have heard, the day before the Wanbaoshan massacre, the Japanese consul met with Chinese farmers under a big tree and said that 2,000 troops would come tomorrow and asked the Chinese farmers to bring coffins to pay for their lives. But the Chinese farmers were not afraid at all. The next day, they bravely resisted. It has become a characteristic. They are the most cruel and despicable nation in the world. After India was destroyed, it was still able to produce great leaders, like Gandhi. In the past, the Hu people entered China and there was only one system in culture. Important News

The Course of the Changes in the Jilin Bureau Under the Control of the Japanese Army 65

Described by Two Professors from Jilin

Tianjin Correspondence: The news that Jilin was reorganized into the so-called "Provisional Provincial Government" under the occupation of the Japanese army is not known in detail between Beijing and Tianjin. Yesterday, Professor Hu Tigan of Jilin University and Professor Jiang Songnian of the Women's Normal School, unable to withstand the stimulation, fled to Tianjin. According to the two gentlemen, this matter is extremely serious. The details are as follows:

On the 19th, Jilin learned that Shenyang and Changchun were occupied by the Japanese army. Acting Chairman and Chief of Staff Xi Qia convened a meeting of provincial committees. On the one hand, he contacted the Japanese consul, and on the other hand, he sent a telegram to the Changchun army not to resist. The garrison in Jilin also began to move out of the city. At this time, there was no news that the Japanese army was attacking Jilin. The Japanese residents in Jilin, including retired soldiers, sent a telegram urging the Japanese army to come to Jilin. The Japanese army notified on the morning of the 21st that they would arrive in Jilin, and then marched from the Jilin-Changchun Road, confiscating weapons along the way. They arrived in Jilin at 6 pm. Xi Qia first sent people to meet the Japanese army several stations away, and he waited at the station to greet them. After the Japanese army entered the city, they occupied various government offices and official silver houses, and put up seals. They were in chaos all night before they could handle it clearly. The next morning, Japanese Division Commander Domen told Xi Qia that although the Chinese army had moved out of the city, it was difficult to guarantee that there would be no accidents, so weapons must be confiscated. Xi Qia then ordered people to handle the confiscation of weapons, but they did not get them back that day, and the deadline was extended to noon on the 23rd. When the time came, they were confiscated. Xi Qia went to see Domen. Domen was suddenly furious and rebuked Xi, saying, "You have not done anything you were told to do. The number of guns confiscated is insufficient, and it was agreed to be completed by 12 o'clock, but you missed the time. Now there is nothing else to say. I have two conditions for you, whether you admit them or not." After speaking, he left the room, and several soldiers entered with guns pointing at Xi. After a short while, Domen entered again and forced him to admit it. Xi Qia reported the confiscation of weapons to the public, but did not mention the two conditions. On the 25th, Xi convened a meeting of various legal groups, and suddenly proposed the reorganization of the provincial government. The Japanese army was severely monitored at the meeting, so it was called a meeting, but no one spoke. That night, two kinds of notices were found on the streets. One was in the name of Xi Qia, the chief of staff of the Border Defense Command, saying that he was responsible for all public security. The other was for maintaining finance, and the person who issued it was the Governor's Office. On the 26th, the so-called outline of the organization of the Provisional Provincial Government was published. The two conditions that Domen forced Xi to admit, one was said to be the reorganization of the provincial government, and the other was said to be the dismissal and transfer of several officials. It is still unknown what happened.

The people of all circles in Jilin now have no freedom to express their opinions. Xi Qia reorganized the provincial government under the Japanese army. The people of Jilin will never admit it, but the post and telegraph are all checked and cannot express their opinions. Now, if there are four or five people walking together on the street, they will be driven away by Japanese soldiers. Therefore, it is even more impossible to hold meetings. If anyone tears off a small piece of the notices posted by the Japanese army, they will be regarded as hindering military operations and will be in danger of their lives. Although the Japanese army did not open fire when they arrived in Jilin, they once stabbed people to death on the street for searching for broken military uniforms. There have been several cases of people being killed inside and outside the city due to various small problems. Japanese military aircraft fly everywhere, firing guns and throwing bombs at will. There is a market not far from the city of Jilin in the countryside. Many villagers gather there. Japanese military aircraft fly over the area and fire at people when they see many people, killing a villager. The Jilin-Hailong Road has suffered even more from Japanese military aircraft. Also, as of the 28th, the Japanese army was still in Jilin, but most of the artillery had been withdrawn, leaving only five, and the cavalry had been withdrawn.

Hu and Jiang described the course of this matter in order to arouse the attention of the government and the national people. What they begged for was only one sentence: "Save Jilin quickly. The later it is, the more dangerous it will be."

Attached are the so-called outline of the organization of the Provisional Provincial Government and the changes of officials announced by Xi Qia as follows:

(1) It is for the matter of notification. It is hereby notified that, due to the current circumstances, in order to seek local security, the Jilin Provisional Provincial Government is temporarily established in the city of Jilin Province after a resolution of the meetings of various legal groups and agencies in the province, which shall have jurisdiction over civil affairs, military affairs, and supervision of judicial affairs, and shall be fully responsible and presided over by the head. All ten articles of the Provisional Provincial Government Organization Outline, in addition to announcing to the people of the province for their information, shall be notified. (Outline) Article 1: The Jilin Provisional Provincial Government shall be established in the city of Jilin Province. Article 2: The Jilin Provisional Provincial Government shall have one head. Article 3: The office of the head shall be called the Jilin Provincial Governor's Office. Article 4: The head shall have full power to administer civil affairs and supervise judicial affairs in Jilin Province. Article 5: The Governor's Office shall have two offices: Civil Affairs and Military Affairs. The organization law shall be determined separately. Article 6: The Governor's Office shall have one secretary-general and several secretaries. Article 7: The Governor's Office shall have the following offices: Finance Office, Construction Office, Industry Office, Education Office, and Police Office. All original agencies in this province that are not subordinate to the above-mentioned offices shall be under the jurisdiction of this office. Article 8: A wooden seal shall be temporarily engraved with the words "Seal of the Jilin Provincial Governor's Office." Article 9: This outline shall be implemented from the date of promulgation. Article 10: Matters not covered may be amended temporarily.

(2) (Official System) After the reorganization of the provincial government, the committee system shall be suspended. The Jilin Provincial Governor's Office shall be established. The official system and positions below the governor shall be as follows: Governor of Jilin Province Xi Qia (formerly Chief of Staff and Provincial Committee). Guo Enlin, Director of the Military Affairs Office (formerly Chief of Staff of the Training Office). Sun Qichang, Director of the Civil Affairs Office (formerly Director of the Construction Office). Pan Enian, Secretary-General, remains in office. Rong Hou, Director of the Finance Office, remains in office. Fu Chuntian, Director of the Construction Office (formerly President of the High Court). Ma Deen, Director of the Industry Office, remains in office. Wang Shixuan, Director of the Education Office. Wang Zhiyou, Director of the Police Office, remains in office. In addition, the subordinate officials have also been slightly changed. 1. Fu Chuntian, President of the High Court, was transferred to Director of the Construction Office. The vacancy was filled by Cheng Yun, a member of the Provincial Committee. 2. Zhou Yuping, Director of the Changchun Municipal Preparatory Office and Negotiator, was transferred to the province and changed to Advisor. The vacancy was filled by Zhang Yanqing, the former secretary of the military headquarters. (It was previously reported that his whole family had died, but it is now known to be untrue.) 3. Zhang Shuhan, Director of the Yanji Municipal Preparatory Office and Negotiator, was transferred to the province and changed to Advisor. The vacancy was filled by Qi Bin, the former county magistrate of Yanji County. Zhang Shushan, Vice President of the Provincial Education Association, was appointed as the county magistrate of Yanji County to fill the vacancy. 4. Ma Zhongyuan, the county magistrate of Changchun County, was ordered to be transferred to the secretary of the Governor's Office in exchange for Zhao Ruwei. 5. Liu Zuyin, the county magistrate of Dunhua County, retreated reluctantly. Liu Xingpei was appointed to fill the vacancy. 6. Wang Baoshan, the former secretary-general of the military headquarters, was appointed as an advisor to the Governor's Office. 7. Liu Guoquan, the director of the Provincial Public Security Bureau, was ill. Zhao Rongsheng was appointed as an agent. It is said that Zhao was formerly the Chief of Staff of the Military Headquarters.
