Establishment of the Harbin Public Security Council 66

Zhang Jinghui Concurrently Serves as Chairman

Recruiting a Thousand-Strong Police Guard

Harbin Dispatch: Zhang Jinghui returned to Harbin on the morning of the 25th from Shenyang. On the day the Shenyang Incident occurred, Zhang sought refuge in the American Consulate. On the evening of the 24th, he was escorted by personnel dispatched by the American Consulate to Changchun, finally returning safely to Harbin. The Special District had been without a leader for many days. Zhang's return provided a leading figure. For the 25th, 26th, and 27th, heads of various organizations held consecutive meetings at the Governor-General's office and Zhang's residence. Emphasizing that maintaining public security and protecting the lives and property of foreigners are responsibilities that cannot be shirked, they convened a meeting on the 27th and decided to organize the "Special District Public Security Maintenance Council of the Eastern Provinces," with Zhang serving as its chairman. The members include Zhao Jinlin, Chief of Staff of the Railway Protection Army Command; Ding Chao, Commander of the Changsui Railway Protection Army; Wang Ruihua, Director of the Special Police Department; Zhang Houhuan, Director of the Railway Police Department; Zang Qifang, Director of the Land Bureau; Zhou Shouyi, Director of the Education Department; and Xu Zhen, Director of the Telephone Bureau. The office is located in the Governor-General's office. Yesterday, a proclamation was specially issued as follows: "In view of the current turbulent situation, this Governor-General, feeling deeply the need to protect the consulates and residents of friendly nations in Harbin and to maintain local security, returned to Harbin from Liaoning on September 24th. Regarding the issue of public security in the entire district, I have convened meetings with various organizations and groups for days, conducting thorough consideration and research. With unanimous agreement, it has been decided to establish the Special District Public Security Maintenance Council of the Eastern Provinces effective immediately, and this Governor-General has been publicly elected as Chairman. All administrative and public security matters will be managed and handled by this Council, which will bear all responsibilities. All merchants and residents of various countries residing in this district must be able to live and work in peace, without any fear or harm. This Council is officially announced to be established on September 27th, with its office located in the Governor-General's office. In addition to notifying the consulates of friendly nations, this proclamation is urgently issued to all merchants and residents of various countries and the Chinese people in this district, so that everyone is aware. Henceforth, everyone must live and work in peace, not listen to rumors, and not alarm each other. This Council will exert twelvefold efforts to maintain local security in this district. This is a solemn declaration." After the establishment of the Council, the first committee meeting was held, deciding that all stationed troops should temporarily retreat outside the city. The Maintenance Council will recruit a temporary police guard of 1,000 men, organized into five brigades, each brigade with four squads, led by Yu Jingtao, Dean of Academics of the Special District Police Academy, to maintain security inside and outside the city. All students of the Police Academy and police trained by the trainers will be incorporated. The future of Harbin's security can be viewed with optimism. However, Japanese residents continue to feign panic, and many have moved back to their country in recent days. On the evening of the 25th, bombs were discovered at the China-Japan Cultural Association in Nangang and the Library in Daoli, resonating throughout the city, causing considerable panic among the citizens. Police rushed to investigate and found that only the stone steps in front of the Cultural Association were damaged, and the library had only a pit blown in the courtyard. It was determined that the Japanese had pre-buried landmines to create terror so that the Japanese army could use it as an excuse to invade Harbin. As the perpetrators were not apprehended at the time, strict precautions were taken afterward in the areas where Japanese residents live to prevent them from employing this tactic again. Since the 25th, Japanese aircraft have flown from Changchun to Harbin for demonstrations three times, distributing leaflets in Japanese and Russian. The aircraft flew extremely low, causing great panic among the citizens. Commissioner Zhong Yuqi lodged a protest with the Japanese Consul today. The Japanese Consul has agreed to forward the protest to the Japanese army in Changchun to cease the arrival of aircraft. (28th)

Japanese Troops Trample the Northeast and the Soviet Union 67

The Ferocious Japanese Harbor Internal Discord

The Soviet Union is Poised to Take Advantage of the Situation

Harbin Dispatch: The Japanese sending troops to the Three Eastern Provinces has been brewing for a long time. Therefore, today's outbreak is not surprising. Regarding opinions within Japan, such as the Seiyukai and Minseito parties, behind which are warlords and capitalists, they are naturally the backbone of those who advocate for this matter. However, the Communist Party in Japan, democratic political idealists, and the Korean Independence Party also express strong agreement with this matter. Initially, we heard this with doubt, thinking it was not credible. Later, according to news from various places, we learned that it was indeed the case. The approval from the Communist Party in Japan and democratic political idealists has other intentions. They believe that a revolution in Japan cannot succeed without an international war. Considering past events, such as in Russia, Germany, and Austria, if the European war of 1914 had not broken out, then Wilhelm and Nicholas, etc., would still be dominating their countries to this day. Therefore, the Communist Party in Japan is also encouraging Japanese warlords to send troops. As for Japan sending troops to the Three Eastern Provinces, the country with the closest international relationship is undoubtedly Soviet Russia. Therefore, before the Japanese prepared their troops and departed, they repeatedly sent people to visit the Russian Consul and the Commander of the Far East to inquire about Soviet Russia's opinion on Japan sending troops to the Three Eastern Provinces. However, the Russians answered with "no opinion." The Japanese could not get to the point. They further asked what the purpose was for Soviet Russia's preparing its Far East military. The Russians remained evasive, but also hinted at considerable sympathy. Within the Russians, there are two points. First, they believe that to communize Asia, a Sino-Japanese war must first occur. This point coincides with the opinion of the Communist Party in Japan. Second, Soviet Russia is very clear about the situation in China, such as the military preparations and internal affairs of the Three Eastern Provinces. The past Sino-Russian disputes of previous years are still on their minds. Furthermore, it is currently during the Sino-Russian Conference. Therefore, they also hope that Japan will send troops, not only to use the troops of others to give the Chinese a major blow to eliminate the long-standing resentment from the 1929 Sino-Russian conflict, but also to suppress the Chinese representatives at the Sino-Russian Conference. Therefore, the Soviet Union believes that Japan's sending troops is a well-executed strategy of using a borrowed knife to kill someone. However, since the Japanese repeatedly probed for Soviet Russia's opinion without success, they were still unable to set their minds at rest. They further sent the Japanese Consul in Harbin, Tahashi Chuichi, to travel to Chita, Boli, Vladivostok, and other places to carefully inspect Soviet Russia's military preparations in the Far East region and what actions the Russians might take. Tahashi Chuichi departed in early September. When he arrived in Vladivostok, it was the day the Japanese military's atrocities began. His return was after the Japanese had occupied Liaoning and Jilin, on September 22nd. However, although Tahashi went to the Russian-controlled Far East region for inspection, the secrecy of military equipment meant that he ultimately could not gain a comprehensive view while rushing around on a train. On the Russian side, since Japan has already sent troops, on the one hand, the aim of suppressing China at the Sino-Russian conference and teaching China a lesson has already been achieved. On the other hand, they believe that since the opportunity has arrived, it should not be easily let go. Therefore, the situation in Moscow is very tense. According to a dispatch from Moscow on September 25th, since the 20th, there have been continuous parades and speeches in Moscow and major Soviet cities, stating that the Russian people must overthrow Japanese imperialism and capitalism, and must avenge the hatred from the Russo-Japanese War of 1905 and Japan's sending troops to Siberia. At the same time, they expressed goodwill towards the Chinese, subtly implying whether Soviet Russia's help is needed, creating a situation similar to that after the Sino-Japanese War of 1894-1895. Therefore, Karakhan, an expert on the East, and cadres of the Red Army boarded a plane on September 24th to inspect the area around Chita and Boli. This is the current situation. The future development of the situation may even trigger a major war in Asia. (September 27th)

Wuhan University Students Petition Against Japanese Aggression 68

Received by He Chengjun

Hankou Dispatch: Since the establishment of the Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association, an anti-Japanese atmosphere has permeated Wuhan, and young students are particularly indignant. The entire student body of National Wuhan University has independently organized an Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association to fight against Japan. On the 3rd, they organized a petition group of over 600 people to petition at the Wuhan Headquarters. The Chief of the Headquarters, He Chengjun, and Chief of Staff Zhu Chuanjing, personally received them. Representatives of the petition group handed a petition letter to He, containing three points: (1) Request the Headquarters to forward a request to the Central Government to declare war on Japan. (2) Wuhan University will organize a volunteer army, and request the Headquarters to issue firearms. (3) Request the Headquarters to increase the number of military instructors in order to intensify military training. After accepting the petition letter, He delivered a speech to the petition group in front of the Headquarters, mainly stating that the Central Government has appropriate measures for the Japanese military's atrocities and is currently in serious negotiations. As for the points in your petition, I will fully accept them and immediately telegraph them to the Central Government. After He finished speaking, the petition group sent a representative, Xie Jia, to deliver a reply of thanks and then marched in an orderly fashion through the streets, passing Jianghan Road, Zhongshan Road, Minsheng Road, Jianghan Customs, and crossing the river back to the school. Also, on the 3rd, the Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association convened a joint meeting of the directors of student affairs from various schools to discuss expanding anti-Japanese propaganda methods. It was decided to organize a large-scale student speaking team. Schools that have already started classes should organize and establish a team before the 8th. Schools that have not yet started classes should organize and establish a team within one week after the start of classes. They are scheduled to depart on Double Tenth Day (October 10th) to give speeches in various locations. (October 3rd)

Implementation Outline of the Anti-Japanese National Salvation Movement in the Education Sector of Hunan 69

Changsha Dispatch: Various sectors of Hunan Province are making great efforts to carry out the anti-Japanese movement. In terms of the public, in addition to jointly establishing a National Salvation Volunteer Team and a Youth Iron Blood National Salvation Corps, they are also actively implementing economic severance. Chinese employees serving in Japanese Qing companies have all resigned. The education authorities now consider young students to be the basic force in the anti-Japanese national salvation movement. They should take advantage of this period to provide anti-Japanese education. They have specially drafted an implementation outline for anti-Japanese national salvation in schools at all levels, which will be earnestly implemented by each school. The outline is recorded below: A. Matters related to teaching: (1) When teaching history, attention should be paid to: 1. The history of Japan's aggression against our country over the years; 2. The tragic cases Japan has caused to us; 3. Japan's conspiracy to annex the Three Eastern Provinces and invade the interior; 4. The crisis within Japan; 5. Analysis of the international situation; 6. The lack of results from previous boycotts of Japan and the determination that should be made in the future; 7. If necessary, facts from points 1 to 4 should be compiled and printed into booklets. (2) When teaching geography, emphasis should be placed on: 1. The geographical relationship between China and Japan; 2. Japan's seizure of our vassal states and territories, and the production of maps to hang up to serve as a warning; 3. Japan's seizure of various rights and interests from our country over the years; 4. Japanese goods flooding the market and absorbing our wealth; 5. The importance of the Three Eastern Provinces in our country's position, as well as the actual situation of their area, products, and population, and the production of maps to hang up; 6. If necessary, facts from points 2, 3, and 4 should be compiled and printed into booklets. (3) When teaching Chinese, emphasis should be placed on: 1. Selecting more texts about anti-Japanese or sufficient to stimulate patriotic sentiment as teaching materials; 2. Giving more essay topics about patriotism and anti-Japanese sentiment; 3. Encouraging students to write more anti-Japanese articles for publication in newspapers or compilation into booklets and publications; 4. Except for novels about patriotism and chivalry, all romantic and lewd novels should be banned. (4) When teaching party doctrine, special attention should be paid to the chapter on nationalism, and facts should be cited to prove it. (5) When teaching music, emphasis should be placed on: 1. Adopting more lyrics that encourage public spirit and raise patriotic thoughts; 2. Strictly prohibiting the singing of decadent and uninspiring lyrics and scores. (6) When teaching physical education, emphasis should be placed on: 1. Elementary and junior high schools should pay attention to Boy Scout training, and senior grades in junior high schools may also implement military training; 2. Female schools above the high school level should focus on nursing training. B. Matters related to moral education: (1) Formulate a oath and have all students swear to resist Japan and save the country (the oath shall be formulated by each school); (2) Formulate a self-reflection form and have each student fill it out once a week to reflect on whether their words and deeds during the week hinder the resistance against Japan and the salvation of the country (the form shall be formulated by each school); (3) Paste anti-Japanese slogans all over the school, and print anti-Japanese slogans on textbook covers, stationery, and envelopes; (4) At the end of each weekly memorial service, anti-Japanese slogans must be shouted loudly; (5) All teachers and staff should eliminate bad habits, invigorate their spirits, and lead students in anti-Japanese work; (6) Students' clothes and supplies should all use domestic goods, and even if it is unavoidable, Japanese goods must not be used. All teachers and staff should set an example; (7) Strictly abide by discipline and avoid romanticism. C. Matters related to group organizations: (1) Anti-Japanese propaganda teams should be organized by students themselves, who, during their spare time, will invite local people (or go to shops, families, and villages) to give speeches on Japan's atrocities against us and various effective methods for us to resist Japan; (2) Ten-person patriotic groups should be organized by students themselves, with every ten people forming a group. If the words and deeds of the members violate the goals of resisting Japan and saving the country, they should correct each other; (3) National Salvation Volunteer Teams should be organized under the guidance of teachers and staff when necessary.

Exuberant Response of Students Studying in Japan to Japanese Aggression 70

Petitioning Ambassador Jiang for Travel Funds to Return Home

Exposing the Japanese Plot of Establishing a "China-Japan Cooperative State"

Osaka Dispatch: Since the danger to Sino-Japanese relations, many Chinese students studying in Japan have successively withdrawn from school and returned home. Most of those remaining are poor, government-funded students. Due to the widespread floods in their motherland this year, and because the Eastern Provinces have been occupied by Japan, government funding from both the north and the south has been uniformly suspended. Hundreds of government-funded students are penniless. Although they urgently want to return home, most are suffering from a lack of travel funds. On the 29th of this month, more than 400 people gathered at the Chinese Embassy in Azabu District, Tokyo, to petition Jiang Zuobin, requesting loans for travel funds to return home, requesting 30 yen per person for travel expenses. They also sent five representatives to meet with Ambassador Jiang to state the amount of their request. Ambassador Jiang said that at 30 yen per person, with 2,000 government-funded students in Tokyo, the total amount would require 60,000 yen in cash, which the embassy was unable to afford, and rejected the request. Thereupon, hundreds of students gathered inside the embassy became agitated and expressed dissatisfaction. Seeing this situation, Jiang personally delivered a speech, promising to prepare ship and train tickets for the students within three days and hand them over to the Liu Student Supervision Office. The students then expressed satisfaction and dispersed.

Since Japan forcibly occupied the Eastern Provinces, Chinese students studying in Japan have been preparing to return home while announcing Japan's intention to invade Manchuria in order to awaken the nation. Yesterday, the Chinese Students' Association in Japan issued a letter to all overseas compatriots, stating that the Japanese cabinet bears the final mission of imperialism. Using the Wanbaoshan Incident as an excuse, it instigated Korean people to hate China. Using the murder of Nakamura as a fuse, it exaggerated the sound of coercion. Finally, it used the excuse of Chinese soldiers blowing up the railway to carry out the military occupation of our Three Eastern Provinces, and even changed the name to the so-called "China-Japan Cooperative State." Its so-called maintaining special rights and interests and resolving long-standing Sino-Japanese issues have proved its true intentions. Our only method to save ourselves from death is for us to rise up and save ourselves. We must unite and make our final struggle, awaken the people of the whole country, strive to fight, and immediately implement economic severance with Japan and declare war on Japan, etc. The resentment of the student community towards Japan is evident from this. (September 30th)

Overseas Chinese Li Shizong of Wakayama Brutally Murdered 71

Corpse Lies on the Side of the Road, No One Cares

News of Missing Overseas Chinese Heard Daily

Osaka Dispatch: Since the Japanese army occupied the Eastern Provinces, Japanese newspapers have been using counter-propaganda to fabricate news of the murder of Japanese residents in China in order to incite anti-Chinese sentiment among the Japanese and encourage them to use retaliatory measures against overseas Chinese. Therefore, overseas Chinese in Japan have suddenly become panicked. When going out, they must either disguise themselves as Japanese or their lives are in danger. Within a week, there have been as many as four cases of overseas Chinese being murdered. In addition to two victims in Tokyo, three days ago, an overseas Chinese man was found hanged in a pine forest under Osaka Prefecture. Without waiting for his relatives to go and collect the body, the Japanese cremated the body immediately, completely destroying the cause and course of the murder, making it impossible to investigate. News of missing overseas Chinese is being heard daily, and most of them are secretly killed by the Japanese. The night before yesterday (the 28th), Li Shizong, an overseas Chinese man from Wakayama (nicknamed Li Daizi, who ran a barber shop), went out to shop and did not return late at night. His colleagues suspected that he had stayed overnight at a friend's house, so they did not look for him. It was not until last night that Li's corpse was discovered by another overseas Chinese man, who immediately reported it to the local barber association. It was then confirmed that Li had been murdered. When reporters heard the news and went to investigate, Li's corpse was still lying on the side of the road, covered in wounds from Han knives and Japanese swords. His brain had been smashed with stones, and blood was everywhere, a horrible sight to behold. Even after the man was dead, several Japanese children were still throwing stones at him from time to time. When asked of the local Japanese police station how the case would be handled, the Japanese police replied that the murder of Chinese people was the result of Japanese people's grievances, and the government could not punish the murderers. As for the corpse, it must be cremated as soon as possible to prevent the spread of the plague, alas. (September 30th)

At the Same Time as Japan Occupies the Eastern Provinces, the Korean Revolution Appears Briefly and Fades Away 72

The Japanese Government Strictly Prohibits Newspapers from Publishing

Tokyo Dispatch: During Japan's recent occupation of the Eastern Provinces, all three divisions of troops stationed in Korea were transferred to Liaoning and Jilin, etc. The security of the Korean territory relies only on a small number of troops and police to maintain it. On the 21st and 22nd of this month, large-scale riots similar to the anti-Chinese movement in July suddenly occurred in Seoul, Incheon, Pyongyang, and other places. Koreans from all over the country rose up and even massacred Japanese residents. It is estimated that more than 20 Japanese people were killed. The Japanese government, in order to address the move of Koreans disturbing the rear at this time of military aggression against China, as it would be unfavorable to both domestic and foreign affairs, swiftly dispatched military police to suppress the riots. They used machine guns to fire everywhere. The Koreans, who had no resistance, were naturally scattered like clouds blown by the wind. In an instant, the revolutionary movement completely failed. Afterward, the Japanese government strictly prohibited newspapers from publishing the news to prevent social unrest. The Korean independence movement has once again appeared briefly and faded away, which is truly regrettable. (September 29th)

Local Correspondence

Suzhou 73

An Eighty-Year-Old Woman is Murdered: Qin Li, aged seventy-eight, of No. 34 Zhuhang River Head outside Changmen Gate, lived separately from her son, Bingkang. The rooms on the east side of Qin Li's bedroom were rented to Wang Laosi and his wife, who were stewards of the Hengfeng Flour Company on Shantang Street. Wang had a nephew, Xu Youliang, who recently moved into Wang's residence. Yesterday morning (the 4th), after Wang got up, he suddenly discovered that Qin Li's bedroom door was wide open, and she was lying in bed with blood flowing from her mouth. She had been dead for a long time. The gold ring she wore on her finger was gone, and the items in the room were in disarray, obviously a case of murder for money. He reported it to the police, who determined that Xu Youliang was a suspect and immediately arrested him for interrogation by the detective team. The investigation is currently underway.

Wuxi 74

A Confucian Husband Commits Suicide by Smoking Opium Out of Fear of His Concubine: Bian Jingui, aged fifty-three, the owner of the Jinchang Cigarette and Sundries Store at No. 79 Xinlu outside Guangfu Gate, is a native of Baoying in Jiangbei. His wife, Zhu, had not given birth to any children. His beloved concubine, Xu, had a son named Guanbao, who is now sixteen years old. Recently, Xu's attitude suddenly changed. She often quarreled with Zhu and completely hid all the property in the house. The cash earned daily in the store was also taken away by her. Jingui, out of fear of her ferocity, dared to be angry but not to speak out and had to endure her actions. A few days ago, Bian, being in dire financial straits, intended to sell the store to the owner of the beef shop next door, stating that the price was 150 yuan. Unexpectedly, Xu learned of the matter and approached the beef shop owner, claiming that she would fight to the death. The matter was not concluded. Under duress, Jingui ingested three mace of raw opium the night before. The next day, his family discovered him and immediately sent him to the Brothers Hospital for treatment, but the poisoning was too deep and could not be saved. He died. The nephew of the deceased, Bian Hongru, claiming that Xu had coerced his uncle to death, reported the matter to the local Public Security Second Branch with Zhu, requesting an investigation. The Wang Branch Chief dispatched the police to detain Xu and send her to the main bureau for interrogation. After the case occurred, the local neighborhood chief, Xi Zhiliang, reported it to the County Court, requesting an autopsy. Upon receiving the report, the Procuratorate sent Prosecutor Yang to the scene yesterday morning (the 4th) at 9:00 AM to conduct an autopsy according to the law. The autopsy determined that the death was indeed caused by poisoning before death. After the autopsy, the prosecutor ordered the deceased's family to prepare a coffin for the funeral. The wives and concubines of the deceased, Bian Zhu and Bian Xu, were also transferred by the Hua Public Security Bureau Chief to the County Court. At 4:00 PM, Prosecutor Yang held a court hearing to question them. As a result, Bian Zhu was ordered to return home, and Bian Xu was detained pending review.

Changshu 75

Villagers Riot and the Public Office is Destroyed: This year's flood in this county is unusually severe. Recently, riotous events have been happening in various districts and townships daily. The day before yesterday, villagers in the first district engaged in rice grabbing in Ouqu. Fortunately, there was police suppression, so no disaster occurred. However, villagers in the tenth, eleventh, thirteenth, and fifteenth districts still believed that there was no hope for the autumn harvest. They gathered at the district office to request rent exemption and emergency relief. Although they were persuaded by the kind words of the district chiefs and the announcement issued by the county government, it was still ineffective. Yesterday (the 3rd), villagers in the thirteenth district gathered again, more than 2,000 people, and rushed into the district office, destroying the telephone first. Various official documents were also discarded and destroyed. That night, the district chief, Hu Yukun, sent someone to the city to report to the county government to request instructions. County Magistrate Tan, considering that the police force there was weak, specially requested the commander of the Weichu militia of the stationed Chang Security Army, to dispatch 30 infantrymen from the first battalion to garrison the Xiaowu City area. The Xiaowu City police were then dispatched to patrol and suppress the riot in various districts. A Robbery and Kidnapping Case Occurs in Luhe Town: In Luhe Town in the eastern part of this county, which borders Taicang, at about 2:30 AM on the 3rd, more than 50 pirates suddenly arrived, each wielding a quick gun and a flashlight. They entered the town from the Yangtze River mouth on three pirate ships, and placed sentries at both ends of the market. Then, they robbed the entire town. As a result, a total of 16 men, women, old, and young were kidnapped, including 13 who belonged to the Taicang border and 3 who belonged to the Yubei border, including Sun Erbao, and Zhang Hongbao and his wife, residents of Sizhou. There was also Sun Jinhai, who resisted the bandits during the robbery and was shot and killed by the bandits. After plundering their fill, the bandits sounded their guns, gathered, disembarked, and fled. During the robbery, the area had specially dispatched people to Dongzhang City and Dongzhou City to report to the police stationed there and to pursue and suppress them, but the bandits had already gone far.

Changzhou 76

Women's Circles Open Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association: Xie Yun, Cheng Peiyue, Wu Cuixian, Qian Fu, and others from the women's circles of Wu County initiated a Women's Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association in the First Park on the afternoon of the 3rd. No fewer than a thousand women from various women's schools and various circles attended. After speeches by the chairman and representatives from various circles, proposals were discussed and decided: (1) Economic severance with Japan, opening of domestic goods stores; (2) Women attending the meeting should each take responsibility for propaganda in their families; (3) Women's schools, etc., should study nursing skills to meet wartime needs; (4) The general assembly should formulate a voluntary letter not to buy enemy goods, and distribute it to women's circles to fill in to show their determination (5) Families should save money and store money to save the country's crisis.

Zhenjiang 77

Yi Zhen Hui Meeting on Accommodation Issues The Jiangbei Flood Relief Association (Yi Zhen Hui) held its sixth board meeting yesterday to discuss the issue of accommodating flood victims. The meeting was chaired by Leng Yuqiu. The following are the discussed matters: (1) It was resolved that the association's transportation boats would cease operations by the Double Tenth Festival, and refugee passes would also expire at the same time. All counties were to be notified to transport refugees as quickly as possible before the deadline. (2) After the shipping industry resumes its regular schedule, four ships should be reserved for the association's use in transporting relief goods. The regular schedules of each shipping company should still include the association's relief goods to various disaster areas. Hereafter, all agencies needing ships should directly contact the shipping association. (3) It was resolved to add two more shelters each in Dongtai and Yancheng, with a limit of accommodating 1,000 people each. One more shelter should be added in Taixian, also with a limit of 1,000 people. All shelters will use the name of the National Government's Flood Relief Committee. The original shelter in Zhenjiang will still use the association's name, and another one will be added with a limit of accommodating 3,000 people, using the name of the National Government's Flood Relief Committee Zhenjiang Shelter. (4) It was resolved that according to the report from Yixing investigator Yang Gongya, there are many refugees scattered in the area without shelter or food, and the water has receded significantly. Given the short window of opportunity, for the sake of current relief efforts, the association will remit 1,000 silver dollars to the chairman of the Yixing Flood Relief Association, requesting them to consider the situation and provide food and lodging or just food, to aid in relief efforts.

Jingguang Grocery Industry Resolves to Eliminate Japanese Goods The Zhenjiang Jingguang Grocery Industry Association, due to the violent Japanese occupation of our Northeast and their ambitious intentions, which has caused the outrage of the entire nation, convened a meeting of all member representatives yesterday to discuss a thorough economic severance from Japan. Six resolutions were unanimously passed: (1) Permanent economic severance from Japan. (2) All stores in the industry must quickly eliminate Japanese goods to erase their presence. (3) If any store in the industry secretly imports Japanese goods again, once discovered, the association will order them to suspend business and request that party and government agencies severely punish them. (4) Now that the industry has implemented the elimination of Japanese goods, it must actively promote the sale of domestic goods to maintain business. (5) Stores in the industry should select the healthiest and most knowledgeable employees to participate in organizing a volunteer army to train and defend the country. (6) One representative should be sent to participate in the anti-Japanese national salvation work in the provincial capital.

Yangzhou 78

Bandits Actually Use Small Boat to Kidnap Victim Zang Tuzu, who runs the Wanhe rice shop and mill in Wantou Town and lives in Shijiazhuang across the river, was visited by a group of bandits at 10 PM on the second night. They came by small boat, rushed into his house, looted everything, and kidnapped his fourth son, Chengru. They then boarded the original boat and left. Anti-Japanese Association Investigates and Discovers Illegally Imported Japanese Goods The Jiangdu County Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association, based on a letter from Zhenjiang reporting that cloth stores such as Yukang, Daren, Mayuanxing, and Tongtaicheng in Yangzhou had ordered a large batch of Japanese goods from Zhenjiang Zhenhe and other treacherous merchants to be transported to Yangzhou, dispatched all its staff, including Standing Committee members Wu Zunyi and others, to investigate near these stores. Committee member Wu, Secretary-General Hu, County Rectification Committee member Chen Shouyan, and Provincial Junior Army Corps Leader Ye Yangyuan led the Junior Army to investigate outside Fuyun Gate. Investigators from the association discovered eight packages of Japanese goods in Yukang at Yuanmen Bridge. It was reported that there were still forty packages en route. Inspection of the goods and invoices confirmed that they were ordered from Zhenjiang Zhenhe. Guo, a Standing Committee member of the Chamber of Commerce, was notified by phone. Guo was also extremely angry and immediately convened a meeting of cloth industry representatives. Twenty-nine representatives attended. Representatives Zhang Jichuan and Wang Xiaoai from the Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association also attended. A public discussion was held on how to handle the situation. Subsequently, another forty-three packages of Japanese goods were discovered, illegally imported by silk and cloth stores such as Yiyantang Hongxing in the city. All goods are stored at the Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association, pending identification before a decision on how to handle them.

Establishment of a Provincial Militia Training Center The Pacification Commissioner's Office, due to the renewed tension of anti-Japanese sentiment after the flood, and the provincial government's concern that bandits might stir up trouble and take advantage of the situation, believed it was necessary to intensify the training of militias in various counties. It requested the Commissioner's Office to establish a militia training center and assign personnel to be responsible for the training. This was specifically brought up at the Commissioner's Office meeting, and it was decided to appoint Wang Chunru as the Director of the Provincial Militia Training Center. A preparatory office will be established immediately to begin work.

Nantong 79

Liang's Troops Deployed to Defend the Coast The infantry and artillery units under the command of Chief Liang, stationed in Nantong, have been ordered to deploy to the coast to set up defenses. Trenches have been dug at various ports. If Japanese warships and sailors arrive in Tong and attempt to land by force, they are to take legitimate self-defense measures.

Thorough Investigation into Court's Opium Case The Nantong Court burned opium on the second day and discovered instances of fake opium and shortages in weight. Public opinion was in an uproar, claiming that the amount of opium involved in the malpractice was over a thousand taels, a serious offense. Various sectors have petitioned the provincial and central authorities for a thorough investigation.

Jiaxing 80

Forced Death Case Occurs in Nan Yan Town Zheng Qiuyan, who runs the Hengchun Lime Shop in Nanyan Town, ordered his live-in granddaughter Chen Yubao (18 years old) to wash his water pipe the other day. Yubao accidentally dropped the pipe head into the river. Qiuyan severely threatened Yubao and ordered her to retrieve it. Yubao, being young, went to the riverbank with tears in her eyes to retrieve it. The water was deep and the current was rapid. After several hours, she still could not find it. The next day, Qiuyan roared at her again. Yubao, with tears in her eyes, went upstairs and hanged herself out of sorrow and indignation. By the time the family noticed, she had already died. People in the town have a lot of opinions about this incident, and it is reported that some are planning to question Qiuyan about it.

Ningbo 81

Fang Ce Comes to Yong to Inspect Forts After the provincial government received a report from the Yongjia County Magistrate stating that a Japanese destroyer, Take-class, had arrived in Wenzhou and was seen passing through Haimen towards Zhenhai, it dispatched provincial commissioner Fang Ce to Yong on the first day to go to the Zhenhai Fortress Headquarters to inspect the forts. He also met with Sun Xingyuan, the Fortress Commander, and Wang Wenhan, the Water Police Bureau Chief, to discuss defense matters. He arrived in Yong at 5 PM yesterday on the Tai'an warship. According to Commissioner Fang, the Japanese warship has not been found in Zhenhai. If Japanese warships do come, since China and Japan have not severed diplomatic relations, our officials should treat them with the courtesy due to friendly nations. The mission of the Japanese Take-class warship, which reportedly has the Chief of Staff of the Japanese Korean Army on board, is to inspect Japanese expatriates in various places. Although there are several Japanese expatriate families in Wenzhou, the sailors on the warship did not land, and their attitude was not unusual. Since there are no Japanese expatriates in Yong, there is no need for the Japanese warship to come to Yong.

Three Traitorous Merchants Paraded Through the Streets The Zhenhai Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association investigated and discovered three treacherous merchants, Zhang Ayu, Sun Yuawan, and Zhu Guilin. It was unanimously decided to parade Zhang Ayu and the other two through the streets to serve as a warning to others. After the parade, Zhang and the others were detained in the county government, to be released after the victory of negotiations with Japan. Sun Yuawan was also fined 120 yuan. A total of over sixty pieces of Japanese goods of various sizes were seized and confiscated for disaster relief.

Shaoxing 82

Tragedy at Magnesium Plant The Sanyi Magnesium Plant, located in Zhentangdian, Shaoxing, experienced a machinery accident at 11 AM on the third day of this month. The plant's machinery cylinder exploded with a loud bang, injuring eight or nine machinists and workers. They were all covered in blood and flesh, a truly terrible sight. The plant hired a boat to send them to the city for treatment.

Special Item

Regulations of the China Anti-Japanese National Salvation Volunteer Corps 83

Article 1: This corps is named the China Anti-Japanese National Salvation Volunteer Corps. Article 2: This corps is based on the determination to sacrifice, cultivate morality, and strengthen the body, with the aim of striving for anti-Japanese national salvation. Article 3: This corps has a creed of ten "don'ts" and ten "musts," the details of which are to be separately established. Article 4: Anyone who agrees with the purpose of this corps and adheres to the creed of this corps may become a member of this corps. Article 5: The general meeting of members is the highest authority of this corps. During the recess, the elected corps affairs committee is the highest authority, executing all corps affairs. The organization under the corps affairs committee will adopt a military-style structure, the outline of which will be separately established. Article 6: This corps has a general meeting of members, a corps affairs committee meeting, meetings of various levels of teams, and class meetings. The general meeting of members is held once every three months. The corps affairs committee meeting, meetings of various levels of teams, and class meetings are held once a week. Extraordinary meetings may be convened when necessary. Article 7: The funds of this corps are divided into two types: annual expenses and temporary expenses. The annual fee is eight jiao per person, which may be reduced or waived for the poor. Temporary expenses will be covered by donations from within or outside the corps when necessary. Article 8: Members who violate the regulations or creed of this corps shall be subject to disciplinary action, the disciplinary regulations of which shall be separately established. Article 9: These regulations shall be implemented from the date of adoption by the general meeting of members. Article 10: If these regulations are not comprehensive, amendments may be proposed at the general meeting of members.

Creed of the China Anti-Japanese National Salvation Volunteer Corps 84

1. Don't buy Japanese goods 1. Must be loyal to the country

2. Don't sell Japanese goods 2. Must use domestic goods

3. Don't travel on Japanese ships 3. Must obey orders

4. Don't work for Japanese people 4. Must abide by corps discipline

5. Don't make foreign-style clothing 5. Must be hardworking and enduring

6. Don't gamble or visit prostitutes 6. Must be responsible in work

7. Don't be corrupt 7. Must love fellow countrymen

8. Don't deceive 8. Must assist comrades

9. Don't watch romantic movies 9. Must cherish reputation

10. Don't read lewd novels 10. Must faithfully adhere to the creed

Organizational Outline of the China Anti-Japanese National Salvation Volunteer Corps 85

Article 1: The organizational system of this corps is as shown in the diagram.

Article 2: Ten people form a class, with one class leader, elected by the members of the class, for a term of half a year, eligible for re-election. Article 3: The class is the basic unit of the corps. Members must have a full understanding of each other, unite as one. It is best if they can automatically organize into classes to join. Article 4: Six classes form a squad, three squads form a company, three companies form a battalion. The number of battalions is not fixed. Each battalion, company, and squad has a leader and deputy leader in charge. Article 5: The appointment and dismissal of leaders and deputy leaders at all levels is executed by the corps affairs committee. Article 6: The company headquarters may have two to four clerks, and the battalion headquarters may have six to ten clerks, all of whom are appointed and dismissed by the directly subordinate leader upon request to the corps affairs committee. Article 7: The corps affairs committee consists of seven members, who publicly elect one person as chairman, and the remaining members are responsible for general affairs, organization, training, propaganda, law enforcement, and documentation, respectively. Each department may have two to four clerks, appointed by the committee. Article 8: The term of office of the members of the corps affairs committee is limited to half a year, but they may be re-elected. Article 9: When a member of each class is absent due to other duties, they should be immediately replaced. Article 10: Detailed rules for each level of team headquarters and each department will be established separately. Article 11: This outline shall be implemented from the date of adoption by the general meeting of members. Article 12: If this outline is not comprehensive, the corps affairs committee may convene a meeting of the leaders and deputy leaders of each level to amend it. Registration office: No. 4, Banbian Street, Xin Jiekou, Nanjing.

Women's Circle of This City Held Anti-Japanese National Salvation Meeting Yesterday 87

Telegraphing All Female Compatriots Nationwide to Economically Sever Ties with Japan

Expanding Work to Organize Volunteer Army and Nursing Corps

The women's circle of this city held an Anti-Japanese National Salvation Meeting at the Public Stadium at 1:00 PM yesterday, resolving to telegraph the National Government to achieve peaceful unification, announce concrete policies towards Japan, telegraph all women nationwide to unanimously economically sever ties with Japan, and organize a women's volunteer army and nursing corps to conduct drills. The details of each item are recorded below.

Attending Organizations Those attending yesterday included the Women's Relief Society, the Chinese Women's Temperance Society, the Chinese Women's Association, the Women's Promotion of Domestic Goods Association, Zhongde Obstetrics, Cihang Midwifery, Huiqun Girls' Middle School, Liangjiang Sports, Jinan University, Shanghai Girls' Middle School, Soochow University, Aiqun Girls' School, Renhe Obstetrics, Dongya Sports College, Shenmei Girls' Middle School, Art College, Minli Girls' Middle School, Daxia University, Peiming Girls' School, Zhende Girls' Middle School, Wuben Girls' School, Chinese Medical College, Chinese Sports College, Biwen Girls' Middle School, Jiangnan College, Gongshi School, Zhi Ren Yong, Chinese Vocational School, Quanzhang School, Huzhou School, Southeast Sports College, Silk Workers' Union, and over 300 other organizations, with over 10,000 people including Pan Tang Guanyu, Liu Wang Liming, Lin Kecong, Wang Xiaoying, and Chen Jingrong.

Meeting Order (1) Entire Body Stand at Attention, (2) Play Music, (3) Sing the Party Song, (4) Pay the Highest Respect to the Party and National Flags and the Portrait of the Premier, (5) Chairman Respectfully Reads the Premier's Will, (6) Silent Tribute, (7) Chairman's Report, (8) Guidance from the City Party Department Representative, (9) Guidance from the Government Agency Representative, (10) Speeches, (11) Discussion, (12) Provisional Motions, (13) Shout Slogans, (14) Adjourn, (15) Play Music, (16) Parade.

The Master of Ceremonies was Wang Xiaoying, the Recorder was Jin Shiyin, the Chief Receptionist was Yang Jingyi, and the Secretaries were Zhao Wenqi and Zhao Gengdi, Fan Aiquan. City Party Department Representative Zhao Erchang, City Social Affairs Bureau Representative Rong Huiren, and Education Bureau Representative Zhou Shang provided guidance. Order at the meeting was maintained by the Fifth Police Brigade of the City Police Bureau and the Boy Scouts from Liangjiang Southeast Sports College.

Chairman's Report Chairman Lin Kecong reported, "Today is the day when female compatriots of the entire city hold an Anti-Japanese National Salvation Meeting. It is also a time of life and death for our country. The number of attendees is so crowded, which shows that the women's circle of Shanghai still has solidarity. Let us quickly and thoroughly resist Japan and use the blood and heads of our 200 million female compatriots to fight to the death with the Japanese invaders. Japan's violence disregards China, which, in other words, disregards the world. If our country does not resist such rampant behavior, our country will inevitably be destroyed by Japan, and the world will become Japan's world. A female friend who arrived in Shanghai the day before yesterday said that after the Japanese soldiers arrived in Shenyang, they raped female students of Fengyong University. A female student who saw this threw a vase at the Japanese soldier, and the Japanese soldier immediately shot the female student to death. Sisters, what do you think after hearing this news? After Japan occupied our three northeastern provinces, it transported a large number of military supplies and warships to China, plotting the independence of the three northeastern provinces and interfering with our national salvation movement. Sisters, it is a dream for us to ask Japan to withdraw its troops. The League of Nations is unreliable; it is a group of imperialist plunderers. If we continue to hold a non-resistance policy, the country will soon be destroyed. Our 200 million female compatriots should all arm themselves and fight to the death with Japanese imperialism. Fellow compatriots, we should unite when the country is in trouble and face the national crisis together. We should use the method of 'sleeping on brushwood and tasting gall' to economically sever ties with Japan, firmly remember the word 'resolution,' and use the spirit of hard work and struggle to save the country."

Representatives' Speeches (A) City Party Department Representative Zhao Erchang said, in brief, "Fellow compatriots, today is the Women's Anti-Japanese National Salvation Meeting. Everyone must remember why we want to resist Japan and save the country. Now our country is about to be destroyed. The 400 million compatriots of China must unite as one and fight to the death with the 60 million Japanese people in the three islands. For example, if 40 Chinese people fight 6 Japanese people, as long as we act in unison, we can always win. At the same time, I also hope that (1) schools will organize volunteer armies, (2) intensify military exercises, (3) resist Japan and strengthen our bodies, (4) resist Japan and learn military affairs, (5) resist Japan and unite our spirits, (6) resist Japan and strictly maintain order, (7) resist Japan and act in unison, (8) resist Japan and pay attention to learning, (9) resist Japan and increase our knowledge, (10) strikes cause learning to be abandoned, so we cannot save the country and resist Japan, (11) strikes make life difficult, so we cannot save the country and resist Japan, (12) strikes cause economic losses, so we cannot resist Japan and save the country, (13) students must work harder and wash away national humiliation, (14) workers must work harder and wash away national humiliation, (15) merchants must promote domestic goods and wash away national humiliation, (16) strict adherence to order shows the spirit of patriotism, (17) obeying discipline demonstrates the spirit of saving the country." (B) Education Department Representative Zhou Shang said, in brief, "Everyone, to resist Japan and save the country, we must do practical work, not just talk empty words. Everyone must recognize that the League of Nations is an imperialist organization and is unreliable. Our policy towards Japan is to treat the symptoms and not waste a single bullet internally, and not spend another bullet externally. We must concentrate our economic and military strength and prepare to fight Japan. The fundamental solution is to have a spirit of hard work and martial spirit, unite as one." Liu Wang Liming, Shu Huizhen, and others also gave speeches in succession.

(3) Request the Ministry of Industry to quickly establish domestic goods weaving factories; resolution passed. The future of the party and the country deeply depends on it. We eagerly await your orders in trepidation. Members of the Kuomintang Zhang Junguang, Zhu Chengzhi, and others, kowtow and salute.

Kui Yanfang Responds to Letter from Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association 93

Huizhong Fish Company

Has Never Imported Japanese Goods

Kui Yanfang responded to the letter from the Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association yesterday, stating: In response, yesterday I received your letter encouraging me with the great cause of patriotism, which I read with awe. Even if I am foolish, how can I not know this? Since you have inquired, I will carefully explain the organization of Huizhong Fish Company and its recent business situation for your inspection. The matter stems from the fact that the 51 pure Chinese fish firms in this port, in view of the past years of mutual infighting among their peers, created an opportunity for foreigners to monopolize the fishing industry. In order to concentrate capital and resist and plug the loopholes, they initiated the organization of Huizhong Fish Company to sell domestic and foreign seafood, not exclusively Japanese fish. Kui Yanfang, entrusted with the heavy responsibility by all the fish industry colleagues who did not abandon him, urged the matter many times, and it was difficult to refuse out of friendship. However, my intention is to plug the loopholes, and the only way to do this is to develop our country's fishing industry. Therefore, before I took office, I submitted this idea to my colleagues for discussion, and they unanimously agreed. Therefore, I resolutely sacrificed everything and reluctantly accepted this responsibility, and declared that the management was a voluntary position, without salary or travel expenses. All the profits of the company would be distributed to the colleagues to show impartiality. The business policy of Huizhong Company is recorded in the declaration of the founding of the company, which is attached for your review. According to Huizhong Company, it was established on June 12 at the Yuye Dunhe Public Office and opened on July 3. What your letter says, according to reports, the fish company was organized at the time of the Wan case to exclusively sell Japanese fish, which is clearly inconsistent with the facts. Huizhong was established before the Wan case, and the goods sold were by no means entirely Japanese goods. When the Wan case occurred, the whole country was indignant. I proposed a proposal not to import Japanese goods, which was unanimously approved by all fish industry colleagues. Therefore, Huizhong has persisted for several months and has never imported Japanese goods. If you don't believe me, there is evidence to prove it. The foreign fish imported into our country is mainly salmon, and salmon used to be all over the market at this time of year, but this year it has disappeared from the market. This is really the result of the fish industry's efforts to boycott. I have persuaded and admonished, and my tongue is worn out, and I am slightly relieved to have achieved this effect. All of the above is the truth, and the nature of the company and my intentions can also be proved by this. Recently, a large number of salmon have arrived in various foreign firms, and people have repeatedly come to negotiate, but I have strictly refused them. It is probably because of this that I have offended people, causing them to spread rumors to confuse your association and vent their personal anger. I am completely voluntary for Huizhong, and what I hope is to guide my fish industry colleagues to develop our own country's fish industry. The management is a voluntary position, and all the company's profits are distributed to the colleagues. Even if I am foolish, how can I dare to risk great disapproval and secretly import enemy goods, benefiting others and harming myself? I am honored to be asked, and I respectfully report to you. I hope that you will disclose the original letter in the newspaper to show the world and clarify the matter. In short, as long as I am alive, I will never act as an accomplice to the enemy and mislead the country. I hope you will understand. Respectfully addressed to the Executive Committee of the Shanghai Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association. Attached is a copy of the Huizhong Fish Company's declaration of founding.

In recent years, the amount of foreign fish imported has been huge. Taking Shanghai as an example, it reaches several million yuan per year, and the right to sell is controlled by foreign merchants, who take advantage of the weakness of competition among our country's fish merchants, manipulate the market, raise prices, and enjoy huge profits. This causes vendors to bear high costs due to mutual competition, and consumers to pay high prices due to foreign merchant manipulation. At a time when our country's fishing industry is not yet developed and people's livelihoods are deteriorating, we in the industry cannot but兼营foreign fish to plug this huge loophole, and how can we bear to let others control us and increase the burden on our people? Realizing that past competition was not a good plan, we are planning for future unity. At the beginning of this year, we once planned, but unfortunately, some were hesitant, so it was not realized. In the early summer, we discussed it with Kui Yanfang, who said with emotion, "The Shanghai fish industry has been disorganized for a long time. If we don't unite, how can we survive? It is not too late to plan now. Although concentrating our strength for direct purchase can prevent foreign merchants from monopolizing and lower prices, the import of foreign goods and the outflow of money are still not fundamental solutions. In the future, we must expand our collective strength to help develop our country's fishing industry and recover great profits. This is the true mission of the fish industry colleagues." Now that the fish industry has this awareness, it is probably the beginning of fulfilling its true mission. If there is anything needed, I dare not spare my efforts to help them succeed. We in the industry are deeply grateful for Kui's words, so we gathered to discuss the organization of Huizhong Fish Company, drafted regulations, and elected Kui as manager. I hope that all of us in the Shanghai fish industry will remain consistent, abandon our individual opinions, eliminate the bad habit of infighting, and unite our hearts and minds to safeguard our industry's rights and seek convenience for the people's food. Our industry's future will hopefully be bright.

Large Number of Overseas Chinese Returning from Japan 94

270 Arrived Yesterday

More than 300 overseas Chinese living in Tokyo, Osaka, Nagoya, and other places, such as hairdressers and kimono merchants, have already left the East and returned home one after another. Yesterday, another 270 overseas Chinese returned from Japan on the Shanghai Maru, unwilling to endure the arrogant attitude of the Japanese. They painfully sacrificed their positions and left Tokyo together, starting their journey back to Shanghai. They arrived in Shanghai at 3:00 PM and landed at the Huishan Wharf. Most of the overseas Chinese who returned this time were from Wenzhou, Zhejiang. After arriving in Shanghai, they will soon return to their hometowns. It is said that a large number of overseas Chinese will leave the East and return home in the near future.

New Naval Aircraft, Jianghe, Manufactured Domestically 98

Test flight yesterday at Longhua Airfield

Piloted personally by Mr. Shen Dexie

Excellent results after fifteen minutes of flight

The two aircraft manufactured by the Aircraft Manufacturing Department of the Ministry of the Navy, one of which was completed at the end of last month and named Jianghe, underwent a test flight at the Longhua China Aviation Corporation airfield at approximately 8:00 AM yesterday. The details are as follows:

Manufacturing Process: The Aircraft Manufacturing Department of the Navy was originally located in Mawei. In February of this year, it was ordered to move to Shanghai and repaired the old buildings of the Jiangnan Shipyard of the Navy at Gaochangmiao West Fort. Construction began in April. All the workers were brought from Mawei, about a hundred people. The director is Mr. Zeng Yijing, who studied in the United Kingdom and has extensive research in aircraft manufacturing.

One Aircraft Completed: The aircraft previously manufactured by the department in Mawei included numbers from Jia to Ji. The one currently being manufactured is Geng. After six months, one aircraft has been completed. Initially, Director Zeng named it Jianggeng, but the Ministry of the Navy ordered it to be changed to Jianghe. All materials, except for the engine, which is an American product, such as wood, paint, and other materials, are all produced in our country. The total price is about 30,000 yuan in Chinese currency. However, its performance is not inferior to imported products.

Test Flight Yesterday Morning: The aircraft underwent its first test flight at the Longhua seaplane field yesterday morning. In addition to Director Zeng Yijing of the department and other important officials of the department, those present included Mr. Shen Xie, Director of the Aviation Department of the Ministry of the Navy, Wang Zhu of China Aviation Corporation, and Mr. Perrin, a Western director of China Aviation Corporation, and over ten others. The workers of the department first transported the aircraft from the manufacturing department to the Longhua China Aviation Corporation for a test flight on the front river. Director Shen piloted it himself. It took off at 9:20 AM, circled the river once, and then left the water surface, soaring in the air for about fifteen minutes before safely landing on the water surface. The results were very satisfactory.

A Glimpse of the Aircraft: The aircraft is very sturdy. The movement of each part, in the air and on the water surface, is very agile. It is an amphibious biplane that can be folded. It can accommodate two people, front and back. It has 165 horsepower and can fly 90 miles per hour. The altitude is over 2,000 feet. The fully loaded weight of the seaplane is 2,460 pounds, and the fully loaded weight of the land plane is 2,250 pounds. The exterior is painted white, and the tail is painted with the national emblem of the Blue Sky, White Sun, and Red Earth. The color scheme is very beautiful.

Mr. Shen's Remarks: According to Director Shen Dexie's statement to the Huadong News Agency reporter, the military and political departments and the navy are now vigorously expanding aviation. However, due to limited funding, rapid development has not been possible. However, expanding the air force is easier than the navy. The Navy of our country currently has about dozens of aircraft. Except for a few imported products, the rest are all manufactured by the Aircraft Manufacturing Department of the Navy in Mawei. They can be used for both military and commercial purposes, and the results are not inferior to imported products.
